     <p> Coniferous trees shroud the trail, snowy boughs creaking beneath the weight of their wintery burden. A single post marks a fork in the ancient road, the signage weathered beyond legibility. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('mH618BGC');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Several caravans are circling a large camp fire on the edge of the cliffs, at the end of a winding steep trail. Any equipment it is wearing or carrying is absorbed or borne by the new form (the couatl's choice)., In a new form, the couatl retains its game statistics and ability to speak, but its AC, movement modes, Strength, Dexterity, and other actions are replaced by those of the new form, and it gains any statistics and capabilities (except class features, legendary actions, and lair actions) that the new form has but that it lacks.       <p> The White Wyverns syndicate are conspiring to assassinate the ruler of the realm. </p>  <p> The syndicates usual gathering venue is <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/X1ruZaji"><strong>"The Flaming Torch Lodge"</strong></a> in <strong>Balaal</strong> </p> 
      <p> The syndicate leader is a <strong>Latilde Ormonde</strong>, a level 10 Elf Rogue.  She has braided red hair, cold dark eyes and long, pointy ears (<em>Nervous</em>). <small>In the pocket: <strong>3 cp</strong>, <strong>an empty vial</strong> and <strong>a key</strong>.</small>
